#wave 1
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] positioned as @e[tag=turn_summon] run summon minecraft:zombie_villager ~ ~ ~ {Tags:["zombie_villager","enemy"],Rotation:[180f,0f],NoAI:1b,ArmorItems:[{},{},{},{id:"minecraft:stone_button",count:1b}],Invulnerable:0b,Passengers:[{id:"minecraft:forest_temple_display",Tags:["hpbar"],billboard:"center"}]}
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=31}] positioned as @e[tag=turn_summon] run summon minecraft:zombie_villager ~ ~ ~ {Tags:["zombie_villager","enemy"],Rotation:[180f,0f],NoAI:1b,ArmorItems:[{},{},{},{id:"minecraft:stone_button",count:1b}],Invulnerable:0b,Passengers:[{id:"minecraft:forest_temple_display",Tags:["hpbar"],billboard:"center"}]}
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=61}] positioned as @e[tag=turn_summon] run summon minecraft:zombie_villager ~ ~ ~ {Tags:["zombie_villager","enemy"],Rotation:[180f,0f],NoAI:1b,ArmorItems:[{},{},{},{id:"minecraft:stone_button",count:1b}],Invulnerable:0b,Passengers:[{id:"minecraft:forest_temple_display",Tags:["hpbar"],billboard:"center"}]}
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] run scoreboard players set @s tick 20
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] run scoreboard players set @s sec 5
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] run scoreboard players set @s sec2 4
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] run scoreboard players set @s min 0
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=1}] run scoreboard players set @s min2 0
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=10}] run setblock 104 -34 71 air
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=10}] run scoreboard players set @s next_wave 0
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=61..,next_wave=..10}] unless entity @e[tag=enemy] run setblock 104 -34 71 minecraft:redstone_block
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,tag=next_wave,scores={next_wave=20,wave=1}] run scoreboard players add @a money 300
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,tag=next_wave,scores={next_wave=20,wave=1}] run title @a subtitle [{"forest_temple":"웨이브 보너스","color":"green"},{"forest_temple":" +","color":"yellow"},{"forest_temple":"300","color":"white"}]
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,tag=next_wave,scores={next_wave=20,wave=0}] run title @a subtitle [{"forest_temple":"웨이브 보너스","color":"green"},{"forest_temple":" +","color":"yellow"},{"forest_temple":"800","color":"white"}]
execute as @e[tag=option,tag=hard,scores={wave=1,wave_option=300}] run give @a yellow_dye[minecraft:item_name='[{"forest_temple":"[ 웨이브 스킵 ]","color":"yellow","bold":true},{"forest_temple":"  [F]","color":"aqua"}]',minecraft:enchantment_glint_override=1]
